`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/update/UpdateManager.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.update

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper
import dev.guardac.GuardAC
import dev.guardac.util.Message
import org.bukkit.Bukkit
import dev.guardac.util.TaskHandle
import java.io.File
import java.net.URI
import java.net.http.HttpClient
import java.net.http.HttpRequest
import java.net.http.HttpResponse
import java.nio.file.Files
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption
import java.time.Duration
import java.util.zip.ZipFile

class UpdateManager(private val plugin: GuardAC, private val pluginJar: File) {

    private val mapper = ObjectMapper().apply {
        configure(DeserializationFeature.FAIL_ON_UNKNOWN_PROPERTIES, false)
    }

    private val http: HttpClient = HttpClient.newBuilder()
        .connectTimeout(Duration.ofSeconds(15))
        .followRedirects(HttpClient.Redirect.NORMAL)
        .build()

    private val stateFile = File(plugin.dataFolder, ".update-state")
    private var task: TaskHandle? = null
    @Volatile private var lastFailureLogMs = 0L

    fun start() {
        val intervalTicks = plugin.configManager.autoUpdateIntervalHours
            .coerceIn(1, 168) * 3600L * 20L
        task = plugin.scheduler.asyncTimer(FIRST_CHECK_DELAY_TICKS, intervalTicks) {
            runCatching(::check).onFailure(::logFailure)
        }
    }

    fun stop() {
        task?.cancel()
        task = null
    }

    private fun check() {
        if (!plugin.configManager.autoUpdateEnabled) return

        val release = fetchLatestRelease() ?: return
        val tag = release.tag_name.trim()
        if (tag.isEmpty() || !TAG_PATTERN.matches(tag)) return

        val known = readState()
        if (known.isEmpty()) {

            writeState(tag)
            return
        }
        if (known == tag) return

        val asset = pickAsset(release.assets.orEmpty()) ?: return
        val bytes = download(asset) ?: return
        if (!looksLikeOurPlugin(bytes)) {
            plugin.logger.warning("[GuardAC] Auto-update: downloaded file for $tag failed validation, skipping.")
            return
        }

        val updateDir = plugin.server.updateFolderFile
        updateDir.mkdirs()
        val staged = File(updateDir, pluginJar.name)
        val tmp = File(updateDir, pluginJar.name + ".download")
        tmp.writeBytes(bytes)
        Files.move(tmp.toPath(), staged.toPath(), StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING)
        writeState(tag)

        plugin.logger.info("[GuardAC] Update $tag downloaded (${bytes.size / 1024} KB) - it will be applied on the next server restart.")
        if (plugin.configManager.autoUpdateNotifyStaff) {
            val msg = plugin.locale.get(Message.UPDATE_DOWNLOADED, "tag", tag)
            plugin.scheduler.global(Runnable {
                Bukkit.getOnlinePlayers()
                    .filter { it.hasPermission("guardac.alerts") }
                    .forEach { it.sendMessage(msg) }
            })
        }
    }

    private fun fetchLatestRelease(): ReleaseDto? {
        val req = HttpRequest.newBuilder(URI.create(RELEASES_URL))
            .header("Accept", "application/vnd.github+json")
            .header("User-Agent", "GuardAC-Updater")
            .timeout(Duration.ofSeconds(15))
            .GET()
            .build()
        val res = http.send(req, HttpResponse.BodyHandlers.ofString())
        if (res.statusCode() != 200) return null
        return mapper.readValue(res.body(), ReleaseDto::class.java)
    }

    private fun pickAsset(assets: List<AssetDto>): AssetDto? {
        val jars = assets.filter { it.name.endsWith(".jar") && it.browser_download_url.startsWith("https://") }
        if (jars.isEmpty()) return null
        val wanted = if (Runtime.version().feature() >= 21) "java21" else "java17"
        return jars.firstOrNull { it.name.contains(wanted) } ?: jars.first()
    }

    private fun download(asset: AssetDto): ByteArray? {
        val req = HttpRequest.newBuilder(URI.create(asset.browser_download_url))
            .header("User-Agent", "GuardAC-Updater")
            .timeout(Duration.ofMinutes(2))
            .GET()
            .build()
        val res = http.send(req, HttpResponse.BodyHandlers.ofByteArray())
        if (res.statusCode() != 200) return null
        val bytes = res.body()
        if (bytes.size < MIN_JAR_BYTES || bytes.size > MAX_JAR_BYTES) return null
        if (asset.size > 0 && bytes.size != asset.size) return null
        return bytes
    }

    private fun looksLikeOurPlugin(bytes: ByteArray): Boolean {
        if (bytes.size < 4 || bytes[0] != 0x50.toByte() || bytes[1] != 0x4B.toByte()) return false
        val tmp = File.createTempFile("guardac-update", ".jar")
        return try {
            tmp.writeBytes(bytes)
            ZipFile(tmp).use { zip ->
                val entry = zip.getEntry("plugin.yml") ?: return false
                val text = zip.getInputStream(entry).readBytes().toString(Charsets.UTF_8)
                text.contains("name: GuardAC")
            }
        } catch (_: Exception) {
            false
        } finally {
            tmp.delete()
        }
    }

    private fun readState(): String =
        runCatching { stateFile.readText().trim() }.getOrDefault("")

    private fun writeState(tag: String) {
        runCatching {
            plugin.dataFolder.mkdirs()
            stateFile.writeText(tag)
        }
    }

    private fun logFailure(cause: Throwable) {

        val now = System.currentTimeMillis()
        if (now - lastFailureLogMs < FAILURE_LOG_THROTTLE_MS) return
        lastFailureLogMs = now
        plugin.logger.info("[GuardAC] Update check failed: ${cause.message}")
    }

    private companion object {
        const val RELEASES_URL = "https://api.github.com/repos/PalassCQ/GuardAC/releases/latest"
        val TAG_PATTERN = Regex("^v[0-9][0-9A-Za-z_.-]{0,30}$")
        const val FIRST_CHECK_DELAY_TICKS = 60L * 20L
        const val MIN_JAR_BYTES = 200 * 1024
        const val MAX_JAR_BYTES = 64 * 1024 * 1024
        const val FAILURE_LOG_THROTTLE_MS = 6L * 3600L * 1000L
    }
}

private data class ReleaseDto @JsonCreator constructor(
    @JsonProperty("tag_name") val tag_name: String = "",
    @JsonProperty("assets")   val assets: List<AssetDto>? = null,
)

private data class AssetDto @JsonCreator constructor(
    @JsonProperty("name")                 val name: String = "",
    @JsonProperty("size")                 val size: Int = 0,
    @JsonProperty("browser_download_url") val browser_download_url: String = "",
)
```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/util/Colors.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.util

import org.bukkit.ChatColor

object Colors {

    private val HEX_PATTERN = Regex("[&<]#([0-9A-Fa-f]{6})>?")

    fun translate(input: String): String {
        val withHex = HEX_PATTERN.replace(input) { match ->
            val hex = match.groupValues[1]
            val sb = StringBuilder("§x")
            for (c in hex) {
                sb.append('§').append(c)
            }
            sb.toString()
        }
        return ChatColor.translateAlternateColorCodes('&', withHex)
    }
}
```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/util/GeyserUtil.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.util

import java.util.UUID

object GeyserUtil {

    private var floodgateApiInstance: Any? = null
    private var isFloodgatePlayerMethod: java.lang.reflect.Method? = null
    private var geyserApiClass: Class<*>? = null

    init {

        runCatching {
            val cls = Class.forName("org.geysermc.floodgate.api.FloodgateApi")
            floodgateApiInstance = cls.getMethod("getInstance").invoke(null)
            isFloodgatePlayerMethod = cls.getMethod("isFloodgatePlayer", UUID::class.java)
        }

        runCatching { geyserApiClass = Class.forName("org.geysermc.geyser.api.GeyserApi") }
    }

    val available: Boolean
        get() = floodgateApiInstance != null || geyserApiClass != null

    fun isBedrock(uuid: UUID): Boolean {

        val api = floodgateApiInstance
        val method = isFloodgatePlayerMethod
        if (api != null && method != null) {
            runCatching {
                val r = method.invoke(api, uuid)
                if (r is Boolean && r) return true
            }
        }

        val gcls = geyserApiClass
        if (gcls != null) {
            runCatching {
                val apiObj = gcls.getMethod("api").invoke(null)
                if (apiObj != null) {
                    val r = gcls.getMethod("isBedrockPlayer", UUID::class.java).invoke(apiObj, uuid)
                    if (r is Boolean && r) return true
                }
            }
        }

        return uuid.version() == 0
    }
}
```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/util/RunningMode.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.util

import java.util.ArrayDeque

class RunningMode(val maxSize: Int) {

    private val addList: ArrayDeque<Double> = ArrayDeque(maxSize)
    private val popularityMap: HashMap<Double, Int> = HashMap()

    var modeValue: Double = 0.0
        private set
    var modeCount: Int = 0
        private set

    fun size(): Int = addList.size

    fun add(value: Double) {
        pop()
        for ((key, _) in popularityMap) {
            if (kotlin.math.abs(key - value) < THRESHOLD) {
                popularityMap[key] = popularityMap[key]!! + 1
                addList.addLast(key)
                return
            }
        }
        popularityMap[value] = 1
        addList.addLast(value)
    }

    private fun pop() {
        if (addList.size >= maxSize) {
            val removed = addList.pollFirst() ?: return
            val count = popularityMap[removed] ?: return
            if (count <= 1) popularityMap.remove(removed)
            else popularityMap[removed] = count - 1
        }
    }

    fun updateMode() {
        var max = 0
        var mostPopular = 0.0
        for ((key, count) in popularityMap) {
            if (count > max) {
                max = count
                mostPopular = key
            }
        }
        modeValue = mostPopular
        modeCount = max
    }

    fun clear() {
        addList.clear()
        popularityMap.clear()
        modeValue = 0.0
        modeCount = 0
    }

    private companion object {
        const val THRESHOLD = 1e-3
    }
}
```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/util/Scheduler.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.util

import org.bukkit.Bukkit
import org.bukkit.Location
import org.bukkit.entity.Entity
import org.bukkit.plugin.Plugin
import org.bukkit.scheduler.BukkitRunnable
import java.lang.reflect.Method
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit
import java.util.function.Consumer

fun interface TaskHandle {
    fun cancel()
}

class Scheduler(private val plugin: Plugin) {

    val folia: Boolean = runCatching {
        Class.forName("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.RegionizedServer")
        true
    }.getOrDefault(false)

    private var globalSched: Any? = null
    private var asyncSched: Any? = null
    private var regionSched: Any? = null

    private var mGlobalRun: Method? = null
    private var mGlobalDelayed: Method? = null
    private var mGlobalRate: Method? = null
    private var mAsyncNow: Method? = null
    private var mAsyncRate: Method? = null
    private var mRegionRun: Method? = null
    private var mRegionRate: Method? = null
    private var mEntitySched: Method? = null
    private var mEntityRun: Method? = null
    private var mEntityDelayed: Method? = null
    private var mEntityRate: Method? = null
    private var mCancel: Method? = null
    private var mTeleportAsync: Method? = null

    init {
        mTeleportAsync = runCatching {
            Entity::class.java.getMethod("teleportAsync", Location::class.java)
        }.getOrNull()
        if (folia) resolveFolia()
    }

    private fun resolveFolia() {
        val pl = Plugin::class.java
        val cons = Consumer::class.java
        val run = Runnable::class.java
        val loc = Location::class.java
        val unit = TimeUnit::class.java

        val globalCls = cls("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.scheduler.GlobalRegionScheduler")
        val asyncCls  = cls("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.scheduler.AsyncScheduler")
        val regionCls = cls("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.scheduler.RegionScheduler")
        val entityCls = cls("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.scheduler.EntityScheduler")
        val taskCls   = cls("io.papermc.paper.threadedregions.scheduler.ScheduledTask")

        globalSched = Bukkit::class.java.getMethod("getGlobalRegionScheduler").invoke(null)
        asyncSched  = Bukkit::class.java.getMethod("getAsyncScheduler").invoke(null)
        regionSched = Bukkit::class.java.getMethod("getRegionScheduler").invoke(null)

        mGlobalRun     = globalCls.getMethod("run", pl, cons)
        mGlobalDelayed = globalCls.getMethod("runDelayed", pl, cons, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType)
        mGlobalRate    = globalCls.getMethod(
            "runAtFixedRate", pl, cons, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType,
        )
        mAsyncNow  = asyncCls.getMethod("runNow", pl, cons)
        mAsyncRate = asyncCls.getMethod(
            "runAtFixedRate", pl, cons, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType, unit,
        )
        mRegionRun  = regionCls.getMethod("run", pl, loc, cons)
        mRegionRate = regionCls.getMethod(
            "runAtFixedRate", pl, loc, cons, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType,
        )
        mEntitySched   = Entity::class.java.getMethod("getScheduler")
        mEntityRun     = entityCls.getMethod("run", pl, cons, run)
        mEntityDelayed = entityCls.getMethod("runDelayed", pl, cons, run, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType)
        mEntityRate    = entityCls.getMethod(
            "runAtFixedRate", pl, cons, run, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType, Long::class.javaPrimitiveType,
        )
        mCancel = taskCls.getMethod("cancel")
    }

    private fun cls(name: String): Class<*> = Class.forName(name)

    private fun ticks(v: Long): Long = if (v < 1L) 1L else v

    private fun handleOf(task: Any?): TaskHandle =
        if (task == null) TaskHandle { } else TaskHandle { runCatching { mCancel!!.invoke(task) } }

    private fun consumerOf(body: Runnable): Consumer<Any?> = Consumer { body.run() }

    private fun consumerOf(body: (TaskHandle) -> Unit): Consumer<Any?> =
        Consumer { st -> body(handleOf(st)) }

    fun global(task: Runnable) {
        if (!folia) {
            Bukkit.getScheduler().runTask(plugin, task)
            return
        }
        mGlobalRun!!.invoke(globalSched, plugin, consumerOf(task))
    }

    fun globalDelayed(delayTicks: Long, task: Runnable): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) {
            val t = Bukkit.getScheduler().runTaskLater(plugin, task, delayTicks)
            return TaskHandle { runCatching { t.cancel() } }
        }
        return handleOf(
            mGlobalDelayed!!.invoke(globalSched, plugin, consumerOf(task), ticks(delayTicks))
        )
    }

    fun globalTimer(delayTicks: Long, periodTicks: Long, task: (TaskHandle) -> Unit): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) return paperTimer(delayTicks, periodTicks, async = false, body = task)
        return handleOf(
            mGlobalRate!!.invoke(
                globalSched, plugin, consumerOf(task), ticks(delayTicks), ticks(periodTicks),
            )
        )
    }

    fun async(task: Runnable) {
        if (!folia) {
            Bukkit.getScheduler().runTaskAsynchronously(plugin, task)
            return
        }
        mAsyncNow!!.invoke(asyncSched, plugin, consumerOf(task))
    }

    fun asyncTimer(delayTicks: Long, periodTicks: Long, task: (TaskHandle) -> Unit): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) return paperTimer(delayTicks, periodTicks, async = true, body = task)

        return handleOf(
            mAsyncRate!!.invoke(
                asyncSched, plugin, consumerOf(task),
                ticks(delayTicks) * 50L, ticks(periodTicks) * 50L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS,
            )
        )
    }

    fun entity(entity: Entity, task: Runnable, retired: Runnable? = null) {
        if (!folia) {
            Bukkit.getScheduler().runTask(plugin, task)
            return
        }
        val sched = mEntitySched!!.invoke(entity)
        val res = mEntityRun!!.invoke(
            sched, plugin, consumerOf(task), Runnable { retired?.run() },
        )

        if (res == null) retired?.run()
    }

    fun entityDelayed(
        entity: Entity, delayTicks: Long, task: Runnable, retired: Runnable? = null,
    ): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) {
            val t = Bukkit.getScheduler().runTaskLater(plugin, task, delayTicks)
            return TaskHandle { runCatching { t.cancel() } }
        }
        val sched = mEntitySched!!.invoke(entity)
        val res = mEntityDelayed!!.invoke(
            sched, plugin, consumerOf(task), Runnable { retired?.run() }, ticks(delayTicks),
        )
        if (res == null) retired?.run()
        return handleOf(res)
    }

    fun entityTimer(
        entity: Entity, delayTicks: Long, periodTicks: Long,
        retired: Runnable? = null, task: (TaskHandle) -> Unit,
    ): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) return paperTimer(delayTicks, periodTicks, async = false, body = task)
        val sched = mEntitySched!!.invoke(entity)
        val res = mEntityRate!!.invoke(
            sched, plugin, consumerOf(task), Runnable { retired?.run() },
            ticks(delayTicks), ticks(periodTicks),
        )
        if (res == null) retired?.run()
        return handleOf(res)
    }

    fun region(location: Location, task: Runnable) {
        if (!folia) {
            Bukkit.getScheduler().runTask(plugin, task)
            return
        }
        mRegionRun!!.invoke(regionSched, plugin, location, consumerOf(task))
    }

    fun regionTimer(
        location: Location, delayTicks: Long, periodTicks: Long, task: (TaskHandle) -> Unit,
    ): TaskHandle {
        if (!folia) return paperTimer(delayTicks, periodTicks, async = false, body = task)
        return handleOf(
            mRegionRate!!.invoke(
                regionSched, plugin, location, consumerOf(task),
                ticks(delayTicks), ticks(periodTicks),
            )
        )
    }

    fun teleport(entity: Entity, to: Location) {
        val m = mTeleportAsync
        if (folia && m != null) {
            runCatching { m.invoke(entity, to) }
            return
        }
        runCatching { entity.teleport(to) }
    }

    private class PaperTimer(private val body: (TaskHandle) -> Unit) : BukkitRunnable() {

        private val self = TaskHandle { runCatching { this@PaperTimer.cancel() } }
        override fun run() = body(self)
    }

    private fun paperTimer(
        delayTicks: Long, periodTicks: Long, async: Boolean, body: (TaskHandle) -> Unit,
    ): TaskHandle {
        val runnable = PaperTimer(body)
        val task = if (async) runnable.runTaskTimerAsynchronously(plugin, delayTicks, periodTicks)
                   else runnable.runTaskTimer(plugin, delayTicks, periodTicks)
        return TaskHandle { runCatching { task.cancel() } }
    }
}

```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/util/TpsMonitor.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.util

import dev.guardac.GuardAC
import org.bukkit.Bukkit

class TpsMonitor(private val plugin: GuardAC) {

    @Volatile var tps: Double = 20.0
        private set

    private var task: TaskHandle? = null
    private var lastSampleNanos = 0L

    fun start() {
        stop()
        lastSampleNanos = System.nanoTime()

        task = plugin.scheduler.globalTimer(SAMPLE_TICKS, SAMPLE_TICKS) {
            val now = System.nanoTime()
            val elapsedMs = (now - lastSampleNanos) / 1_000_000.0
            lastSampleNanos = now
            if (elapsedMs > 0.0) {
                val measured = (SAMPLE_TICKS * 1000.0 / elapsedMs).coerceIn(0.0, 20.0)
                tps = tps * (1.0 - EMA_ALPHA) + measured * EMA_ALPHA
            }
        }
    }

    fun stop() {
        task?.cancel()
        task = null
        tps = 20.0
    }

    private companion object {
        const val SAMPLE_TICKS = 100L
        const val EMA_ALPHA    = 0.4
    }
}

```

`src/main/kotlin/dev/guardac/violation/ViolationLog.kt`:

```kt
/*
 * This file is part of GuardAC - https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
 * Copyright (C) 2026 GuardAC
 *
 * GuardAC is free software: you can redistribute it and/or modify
 * it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
 * the Free Software Foundation, either version 3 of the License, or
 * (at your option) any later version.
 *
 * GuardAC is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
 * but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
 * MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
 * GNU General Public License for more details.
 *
 * You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
 * along with this program. If not, see <http://www.gnu.org/licenses/>.
 */

package dev.guardac.violation

import java.time.Instant
import java.time.ZoneId
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter
import java.util.UUID
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentLinkedDeque

class ViolationLog {

    data class Entry(
        val uuid: UUID,
        val playerName: String,
        val checkName: String,
        val vl: Int,
        val probability: Double,
        val buffer: Double,
        val verbose: String,
        val actions: List<String>,
        val time: Instant = Instant.now(),
    ) {
        fun format(): String {
            val timeStr = FORMATTER.format(time)
            val prob = "%.2f".format(probability * 100)
            return "§8[$timeStr] §e${playerName} §8| §7${checkName} §8| §7VL:${vl} §8| §7${prob}% §8| §7${verbose}"
        }

        private companion object {
            val FORMATTER: DateTimeFormatter =
                DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("HH:mm:ss").withZone(ZoneId.systemDefault())
        }
    }

    private val entries = ConcurrentLinkedDeque<Entry>()

    fun record(entry: Entry) {
        entries.addFirst(entry)
        while (entries.size > MAX_ENTRIES) entries.pollLast()
    }

    fun recent(limit: Int = MAX_ENTRIES): List<Entry> =
        entries.take(limit)

    fun forPlayer(uuid: UUID, limit: Int = 20): List<Entry> =
        entries.filter { it.uuid == uuid }.take(limit)

    fun clear() = entries.clear()

    fun size(): Int = entries.size

    private companion object {
        const val MAX_ENTRIES = 50
    }
}
```

```yml
# ── GuardAC ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Quick start: paste your key into ai.api-key below, then run /guard reload.
# Get a key: https://guardac.net
#
# Note: these comments are fixed text and stay in English. The `locale` option
# below switches everything the plugin SAYS (staff alerts, command output,
# player messages) between languages.

config-version: 32

# Language of all plugin messages: en | ru
locale: "en"

# Name of this server, shown in your web dashboard, in staff alerts and in
# cross-server messages. Give each of your servers its own name (e.g. "survival",
# "bedwars-1"). Leave empty to auto-name it srv-<port>.
server-name: ""

ai:
  # Master switch for the AI detection.
  enabled: true
  # GuardAC backend address. Domain only - the API path is added automatically.
  server: "https://guardac.net"
  # Your personal API key from the dashboard at https://guardac.net
  api-key: "PASTE-YOUR-GUARDAC-KEY"
  # How many movement ticks make one analysis window. 40 = ~2 seconds of combat.
  # DO NOT CHANGE. The neural network is trained on a 40-tick window and any
  # other value makes its verdicts unreliable.
  sequence: 40
  # Give up on a backend request after this many seconds.
  timeout-seconds: 5
  # true = staff get alerts but nobody is punished automatically.
  # Recommended while you are still evaluating the detections.
  only-alert: false

alerts:
  # Show a hit to staff when the AI is at least this confident (0-100).
  min-hit-confidence: 75
  # One alert per this many suspicious hits: x3, then x6, x9 and so on.
  # A lone random spike below the bar stays silent.
  min-hits: 3
  # Also print alerts to the server console.
  print-to-console: true
  # Sound played to staff on an alert. A soft, pleasant note-block chime by
  # default; any Bukkit Sound name works (e.g. ENTITY_EXPERIENCE_ORB_PICKUP).
  sound:
    enabled: true
    type: "BLOCK_NOTE_BLOCK_PLING"
    volume: 0.8
    pitch: 1.5

# Violation levels slowly expire so an old flag does not haunt a player forever.
vl-decay:
  enabled: true
  # Check every N seconds...
  interval-seconds: 60
  # ...and remove this many VL from everyone.
  amount: 1
  # Do not decay while the player is actively fighting.
  skip-in-combat: true

punishment:
  # Ignore repeat punishments for the same player within this window (ms).
  # Protects against a burst of flags stacking several bans in one fight.
  cooldown-ms: 5000

animations:
  # Visual show played on the cheater right before a ban (see punishments.yml).
  enabled: true
  # Play a random animation before any real punishment command automatically,
  # even when no [animation] step is configured for that level.
  auto-on-ban: true
  # Animation used when a type is not specified explicitly:
  # pig | explode | particles | lightning | vortex | meteor | cage
  default: particles
  # Length of the show, in ticks (20 = 1 second).
  duration-ticks: 60
  # Particle type and density for the "particles" animation.
  particle: FLAME
  particle-count: 30
  # Play sound effects during the show.
  sound: true
  # An animation always ends with a ban. If the punishment level that fired
  # has no command of its own (only [alert] / [log]), this ban is issued
  # automatically after the show. Time formats: 30d / 12h / 45m; "" = permanent.
  fallback-ban-time: "30d"
  fallback-ban-reason: "Cheating software detected (GuardAC)"

# Commands run when staff click a player in /guard menu.
# Placeholders: <admin>, <target>. Empty list = spectator mode + teleport.
menu:
  click-commands: []

# Learns each player's personal aim style and alerts when it suddenly changes
# mid-session (cheat toggled on, or someone else on the account). Alert only,
# never punishes by itself.
fingerprint:
  enabled: true

geyser:
  # Skip Bedrock (phone/console) players - their aim works differently
  # and must not be judged by a model trained on PC players.
  exempt-bedrock: true

# Automatic plugin updates from the official GuardAC releases.
auto-update:
  # When a new version is published, download it in the background and stage it
  # so the server applies it on the next restart. No files to copy by hand.
  enabled: true
  # How often to look for a new version, in hours.
  check-interval-hours: 6
  # Tell online staff (guardac.alerts permission) when an update was downloaded.
  notify-staff: true

# WorldGuard regions where detection is disabled (arenas with special rules etc).
worldguard:
  enabled: false
  disabled-regions:
    - "world:spawn"

# Forget combat state after this long without a fight.
combat-reset:
  enabled: true
  after-seconds: 60

# Soft, temporary in-combat measures against suspects - not a punishment.
# A suspect's attack speed drops while suspicion is high, and a repeated
# detection briefly blocks their damage. Everything recovers on its own.
combat-suppression:
  enabled: false

# /guard scan <player> - on-demand deep check by staff.
deep-scan:
  # How many combat windows to collect for the verdict.
  windows: 8
  # Give up if the player stops fighting for this long.
  timeout-seconds: 120

# Share detection alerts between all servers using this API key - no proxy
# needed, the GuardAC backend relays them. A flag on one server shows up for
# staff on every other one (staff toggle it with /guard crossserver).
cross-server:
  enabled: false
  # How often to ask the backend for new alerts, in seconds.
  poll-seconds: 10

# Moderation from the web dashboard (guardac.net): a ban issued on the site is
# picked up by every server using this API key and applied locally.
web-commands:
  enabled: true
  # How often to check for new commands, in seconds.
  poll-seconds: 15
  # Which ban system executes web bans:
  #   auto        - use LiteBans if installed, else AdvancedBan, else vanilla /ban
  #   vanilla     - always use the built-in Minecraft ban list
  #   litebans    - always use LiteBans
  #   advancedban - always use AdvancedBan
  #   command     - run the custom commands below
  ban-bridge: "auto"
  # Custom commands for ban-bridge: "command". Placeholders:
  # {player} {reason} {minutes} {duration} (duration like "30d").
  ban-command: ""
  tempban-command: ""
  unban-command: ""

# GuardAC global reputation network: detections on other servers using GuardAC
# are visible to you, and yours help everyone else.
reputation:
  enabled: true
  # Report confirmed detections to the network.
  report: true
  # Warn staff when a joining player has detections elsewhere.
  check-on-join: true
  # ...but only if they have at least this many.
  alert-threshold: 1
```

```yml
hologram:
  enabled: true
  update-interval-ticks: 5
  view-distance: 40.0
  # Height of the lowest feed line above the player's feet. The feed grows
  # upwards, so it never overlaps the regular nickname.
  y-offset: 2.6

  # Bottom line (closest to the nickname). Placeholder {AVG} = average
  # probability in % (colored).
  header: "&7AVG {AVG}"

  # Feed of recent hits ABOVE the AVG line, newest on top.
  # Placeholder {PROB} = hit probability in 0.9999 format (colored).
  hit-format: "&8○ {PROB}"

  # How many recent hits to show (0 = only the AVG line).
  max-hits: 5

  # Distance between lines in blocks.
  line-height: 0.26

  # Number colors depending on the probability %:
  #   0-35%   -> green (&a)
  #   35-50%  -> light green (&2)
  #   50-80%  -> orange (&6)
  #   80-100% -> red (&c)
  colors:
    low: "&a"           # 0-35%
    medium: "&2"        # 35-50%
    high: "&6"          # 50-80%
    critical: "&c"      # 80-100%
    thresholds:
      medium: 0.35
      high: 0.50
      critical: 0.80
```

`src/main/resources/monitor.yml`:

```yml
# Colors used by /guard monitor and the /guard prob HUD.
# A probability below "low" is green, below "medium" yellow, and so on.
monitor:
  colors:
    low: "&a"
    medium: "&e"
    high: "&6"
    critical: "&c"
  # Thresholds in % where each color starts.
  thresholds:
    low: 35
    medium: 55
    high: 85

```

`src/main/resources/plugin.yml`:

```yml
name: GuardAC
version: '${version}'
main: dev.guardac.GuardAC
api-version: 1.16
folia-supported: true
authors:
  - Palass
website: https://github.com/PalassCQ/GuardAC
description: GuardAC - AI-powered anticheat with a TCN combat model. One smart check, zero clutter.
depend:
  - packetevents
softdepend:
  - WorldGuard
  - floodgate
  - Geyser-Spigot

commands:
  guard:
    description: GuardAC main administration command
    usage: /guard <help|alerts|monitor|profile|reload|suspicious|menu|debug|prob|exempt|reset|punish|scan|stats|log|history|results|crossserver>
    aliases: [gac, guardac]
  guarddc:
    description: GuardAC dataset collection for AI training
    usage: /guarddc <start|stop|cancel|status> [player] [LEGIT|CHEAT] [details...]
    permission: guardac.datacollect
    aliases: [gdc]

permissions:
  # Master permission - grants every sub-command permission below. Give this to
  # a full admin; grant individual guardac.command.* nodes for limited staff
  # (e.g. a helper who may ONLY use /guard monitor and /guard suspicious).
  guardac.admin:
    description: Full access to all GuardAC administration commands
    default: op
    children:
      guardac.command.help: true
      guardac.command.reload: true
      guardac.command.alerts: true
      guardac.command.monitor: true
      guardac.command.profile: true
      guardac.command.suspicious: true
      guardac.command.menu: true
      guardac.command.debug: true
      guardac.command.prob: true
      guardac.command.exempt: true
      guardac.command.reset: true
      guardac.command.punish: true
      guardac.command.scan: true
      guardac.command.stats: true
      guardac.command.crossserver: true
      guardac.command.log: true
      guardac.command.history: true
      guardac.command.results: true
  guardac.command.help:        { description: Show GuardAC help,          default: op }
  guardac.command.reload:      { description: Reload GuardAC config,       default: op }
  guardac.command.alerts:      { description: Toggle receiving alerts,     default: op }
  guardac.command.monitor:     { description: Live combat monitor,         default: op }
  guardac.command.profile:     { description: View a player's AI profile,  default: op }
  guardac.command.suspicious:  { description: List suspicious players,     default: op }
  guardac.command.menu:        { description: Open the suspects menu,      default: op }
  guardac.command.debug:       { description: Debug a player's rotation,   default: op }
  guardac.command.prob:        { description: Live probability actionbar,  default: op }
  guardac.command.exempt:      { description: Exempt players from checks,  default: op }
  guardac.command.reset:       { description: Reset a player's VL,         default: op }
  guardac.command.punish:      { description: Manually punish a player,    default: op }
  guardac.command.scan:        { description: Deep-scan a player,          default: op }
  guardac.command.stats:       { description: View server AC stats,        default: op }
  guardac.command.crossserver: { description: Toggle cross-server alerts,  default: op }
  guardac.command.log:         { description: View the violation log,      default: op }
  guardac.command.history:     { description: View punishment history,     default: op }
  guardac.command.results:     { description: AI result history window,    default: op }
  guardac.alerts:
    description: Receive cheat detection alerts
    default: op
  guardac.bypass:
    description: Bypass all GuardAC checks
    default: false
  guardac.datacollect:
    description: Access to dataset collection commands
    default: op

```

`src/main/resources/punishments.yml`:

```yml
# ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
# ║                  GuardAC · Punishments                        ║
# ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
#
# GuardAC has a single check - the neural "AI" aim analysis. This file decides
# what happens at each violation level (VL). A player gains VL with every
# confirmed detection and loses it over time (config.yml -> vl-decay).
#
# Placeholders usable in commands:
#   <player>          - player name
#   <check>           - check name (always AI)
#   <vl>              - current violation level
#   <verbose>         - model confidence, e.g. "94%"
#
# Special actions:
#   [alert]           - notify staff
#   [log]             - write to console
#   [reset]           - reset the group's VL
#   [wait] <time>     - pause the chain (2s, 40t, 500ms)
#   [broadcast] <msg> - message to all players
#   [animation] <type>- visual show BEFORE the next action:
#                       pig | explode | particles | lightning | vortex | meteor | cage
#                       (settings in config.yml -> animations)
#   [ban] <time> <reason> - ban through your ban system (LiteBans / AdvancedBan /
#                       vanilla, see config.yml -> web-commands.ban-bridge).
#                       Time like 30d / 12h / 45m; omit it for a permanent ban.
#                       Works on every server - no tempban plugin required.
#   <command>         - run as console
#
# `actions` are grouped by VL. The nearest level BELOW fires: at VL=4 the
# block "3" runs. A random animation plays automatically before any real
# command (config.yml -> animations.auto-on-ban), no [animation] line needed.
#
# This file is only about commands on specific violation levels. Early staff
# warnings and soft in-combat measures live in config.yml instead - they have
# no commands, only thresholds and switches.

Punishments:

  AI:
    checks:
      - "AI"
    actions:
      1:
        - "[alert]"
        - "[log]"
      3:
        - "[alert]"
        - "[log]"
        - "[broadcast] &#22D3EE▍ &#AEB8C4GuardAC &8» &#FF4D6D<player> &7banned for &#AEB8C430 days &8(&7VL:&#AEB8C4<vl>&8)"
        - "[ban] 30d GuardAC Detection (VL:<vl>)"
      5:
        - "[alert]"
        - "[log]"
        - "[broadcast] &#22D3EE▍ &#AEB8C4GuardAC &8» &#FF4D6D<player> &7banned for &#AEB8C430 days &8(&7VL:&#AEB8C4<vl>&8)"
        - "[ban] 30d GuardAC Detection (VL:<vl>)"
      7:
        - "[alert]"
        - "[log]"
        - "[broadcast] &#22D3EE▍ &#AEB8C4GuardAC &8» &#FF4D6D<player> &7banned for &#AEB8C430 days &8(&7VL:&#AEB8C4<vl>&8)"
        - "[ban] 30d GuardAC Detection (VL:<vl>)"
      10:
        - "[alert]"
        - "[log]"
        - "[broadcast] &#22D3EE▍ &#AEB8C4GuardAC &8» &#FF4D6D<player> &cbanned permanently &8(&7VL:&#AEB8C4<vl>&8)"
        # An animation plays automatically before the ban (animations.auto-on-ban).
        # Want a specific one instead of random? Add here: "[animation] pig".
        - "[ban] Cheating (GuardAC VL:<vl>)"
        - "[reset]"

```
